    16	
    17	package model
    18	
    19	import (
    20	        "k8s.io/kops/upup/pkg/fi"
    21	        "k8s.io/kops/upup/pkg/fi/nodeup/nodetasks"
    22	)
    23	
    24	// NvidiaBuilder installs the Nvidia driver and runtime.
    25	type NvidiaBuilder struct {
    26	        *NodeupModelContext
    27	}
    28	
    29	var _ fi.NodeupModelBuilder = &NvidiaBuilder{}
    30	
    31	// Build is responsible for installing packages.
    32	func (b *NvidiaBuilder) Build(c *fi.NodeupModelBuilderContext) error {
    33	        if b.InstallNvidiaRuntime() && b.Distribution.IsUbuntu() {
    34	                c.AddTask(&nodetasks.AptSource{
    35	                        Name:    "nvidia-container-toolkit",
    36	                        Keyring: "https://nvidia.github.io/libnvidia-container/gpgkey",
    37	                        Sources: []string{
    38	                                "deb https://nvidia.github.io/libnvidia-container/stable/deb/$(ARCH) /",
    39	                        },
    40	                })
    41	                c.AddTask(&nodetasks.Package{Name: "nvidia-container-toolkit"})
    42	                c.AddTask(&nodetasks.Package{Name: b.NodeupConfig.NvidiaGPU.DriverPackage})
    43	        }
    44	        return nil
    45	}

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on /testbed/hooks/nvidia-device-plugin/README.md:
     1	# NVIDIA GPU Driver and DevicePlugin Installation
     2	
     3	## Summary
     4	
     5	This kops hook container may be used to enable nodes with GPUs to work with
     6	Kubernetes.  It is targeted specifically for AWS GPU [instance
     7	types](https://aws.amazon.com/ec2/instance-types/).
     8	
     9	It installs the following from web sources.
    10	
    11	1. [NVIDIA Device Drivers](http://www.nvidia.com/Download/index.aspx)
    12	2. [CUDA Libraries](https://developer.nvidia.com/cuda-downloads)
    13	3. [nvidia-docker](https://github.com/NVIDIA/nvidia-docker)
    14	4. [docker-ce](https://www.docker.com/community-edition)
    15	
    16	Using this hook indicates that you agree to the NVIDIA
    17	[license](http://www.nvidia.com/content/DriverDownload-March2009/licence.php?lang=us).
    18	
    19	## How it works
    20	
    21	* This kops hook container runs on a kubernetes node upon every boot.
    22	* It installs onto the host system a systemd oneshot service unit
    23	  `nvidia-device-plugin.service` along with setup scripts.
    24	* The systemd unit `nvidia-device-plugin.service` runs and executes the setup
    25	  scripts in the host directory `/nvidia-device-plugin`.
    26	* The scripts install the NVIDIA device drivers, CUDA libs, nvidia-docker along
    27	  with the matching version of docker-ce.
    28	* The scheduling of work in a separate systemd unit outside of this kops hook
    29	  is required because it is not possible to upgrade docker-ce on the host from
    30	  within a docker container.
    31	
    32	## Prerequisites
    33	
    34	Although this hook *may* work among many combinatorial versions of software and
    35	images, it has only been tested with the following:
    36	
    37	* kops: **1.9**, **1.15.0**
    38	* kubernetes: 1.10, **1.11**, **1.15.5**
    39	* OS Image: **`kope.io/k8s-1.10-debian-stretch-amd64-hvm-ebs-2018-05-27`**, **`kope.io/k8s-1.15-debian-stretch-amd64-hvm-ebs-2020-01-17`**
    40	  * This is most certainly not the default image for kops.  The OS image must
    41	    be explicitly overridden in the cluster or instancegroup spec.
    42	  * Debian stretch is needed because `nvidia-docker` requires a newer version
    43	    of `docker-ce >= 18.0`, which is not available in the Debian jessie package
    44	    repository.  In addition, the Debian jessie kernel was compiled with gcc-7,
    45	    while the system packages install gcc-4, thus making the nvidia driver
    46	    compilation fail.
    47	* cloud: **AWS**
    48	  * This hook will only work on AWS at this moment.
    49	  * This is due to the fact that it uses an AWS discovery mechanism to
    50	    determine node instancetype, and subsequently install the correct drivers and
    51	    configure the optimal settings for the GPU chipsets.
    52	
    53	### Test Matrix
    54	
    55	This kOps hook was developed against the following version combinations.
    56	
    57	| Kops Version  | Kubernetes Version | GPU Mode     | OS Image |
    58	| ------------- | ------------------ | ------------ | -------- |
    59	| 1.15.0        | 1.15.5             | deviceplugin | kope.io/k8s-1.15-debian-stretch-amd64-hvm-ebs-2020-01-17
    60	| 1.10-beta.1   | 1.10               | deviceplugin | kope.io/k8s-1.10-debian-stretch-amd64-hvm-ebs-2018-05-27
    61	| 1.9.1         | 1.11               | deviceplugin | kope.io/k8s-1.10-debian-stretch-amd64-hvm-ebs-2018-05-27
    62	| 1.9.1         | 1.10               | legacy       | kope.io/k8s-1.10-debian-stretch-amd64-hvm-ebs-2018-05-27
    63	
    64	### About the Docker Image
    65	
    66	- For CUDA 10.0, run `DOCKER_REGISTRY= make image push` with the desired registry to self-host the docker image.
    67	- For CUDA 9.1, the image is already hosted according to the InstanceGroup spec example but can be mirrored elsewhere.
    68	
    69	## Using this DevicePlugin
    70	
    71	### Create a Cluster with GPU Nodes
    72	
    73	```bash
    74	kops create cluster \
    75	  --name gpu.example.k8s.local \
    76	  --zones us-east-1c \
    77	  --node-size p2.xlarge \
    78	  --node-count 1 \
    79	  --image kope.io/k8s-1.15-debian-stretch-amd64-hvm-ebs-2020-01-17 \
    80	  --kubernetes-version 1.15.5
    81	```
    82	
    83	### Enable the Kops Installation Hook and DevicePlugins
    84	
    85	This should be safe to do for all machines, because the hook auto-detects if
    86	the machine is an AWS GPU instancetype and will NO-OP otherwise. Choose
    87	between the DevicePlugin GPU Mode or Legacy Accelerators GPU Mode.
    88	
    89	#### (Preferred) DevicePlugin GPU Mode
    90	
    91	This mode is:
    92	
    93	* Required for kubernetes >= 1.11.0
    94	* Optional for 1.8.0 =< kubernetes <= 1.11.0
    95	
    96	For Kubernetes >= 1.11.0 or clusters supporting DevicePlugins
    97	
    98	```yaml
    99	# > kops edit instancegroup nodes
   100	# CUDA 10.0
   101	spec:
   102	  image: kope.io/k8s-1.15-debian-stretch-amd64-hvm-ebs-2020-01-17
   103	  hooks:
   104	  - execContainer:
   105	      image: DOCKER_REGISTRY/nvidia-device-plugin:0.2.0-cuda10.0 # Replace DOCKER_REGISTRY with the registry used to host the image
   106	
   107	# CUDA 9.1
   108	spec:
   109	  image: kope.io/k8s-1.10-debian-stretch-amd64-hvm-ebs-2018-05-27
   110	  hooks:
   111	  - execContainer:
   112	      image: dcwangmit01/nvidia-device-plugin:0.1.0
   113	
   114	### The settings below are only necessary for kubernetes <= 1.11.0, where
   115	###   deviceplugins are not enabled by default.
   116	# kubelet:
   117	#   featureGates:
   118	#     # Enable DevicePlugins
   119	#     DevicePlugins: "true"
   120	#     # Disable Accelerators (may interfere with DevicePlugins)
   121	#     Accelerators: "false"
   122	```
   123	
   124	#### (Deprecated) Legacy Accelerators GPU Mode
   125	
   126	The legacy `accelerator`
   127	GPU mode is equivalent to the original [GPU hook](/docs/gpu.md).
   128	Accelerators are deprecated in `Kubernetes >= 1.11.0`.
   129	
   130	```yaml
   131	# > kops edit instancegroup nodes
   132	
   133	spec:
   134	  image: kope.io/k8s-1.10-debian-stretch-amd64-hvm-ebs-2018-05-27
   135	  hooks:
   136	  - execContainer:
   137	      image: dcwangmit01/nvidia-device-plugin:0.1.0
   138	      environment:
   139	        NVIDIA_DEVICE_PLUGIN_MODE: legacy
   140	  kubelet:
   141	    featureGates:
   142	      # Disable DevicePlugins (may interfere with DevicePlugins)
   143	      DevicePlugins: "false"
   144	      # Enable Accelerators
   145	      Accelerators: "true"
   146	```
   147	
   148	### Update the cluster
   149	
   150	```bash
   151	kops update cluster gpu.example.k8s.local --yes
   152	kops rolling-update cluster gpu.example.k8s.local --yes
   153	```
   154	
   155	### Deploy the Daemonset for the NVIDIA DevicePlugin
   156	
   157	Only for DevicePlugin GPU Mode, load the deviceplugin daemonset for your
   158	specific environment. This is not required for the Legacy Accelerators GPU
   159	Mode.
   160	
   161	```bash
   162	kubectl create -f https://raw.githubusercontent.com/NVIDIA/k8s-device-plugin/1.0.0-beta5/nvidia-device-plugin.yml
   163	
   164	# (Optional) Set permissive toleration to allow daemonset to run anywhere.
   165	#   By default this is permissive in case you have tainted your GPU nodes.
   166	kubectl patch daemonset nvidia-device-plugin-daemonset --namespace kube-system \
   167	  -p '{ "spec": { "template": { "spec": { "tolerations": [ { "operator": "Exists" } ] } } } }'
   168	```
   169	
   170	### Validate that GPUs are Working
   171	
   172	#### Deploy a Test Pod
   173	
   174	```bash
   175	# CUDA 10.0
   176	cat << EOF | kubectl apply -f -
   177	apiVersion: v1
   178	kind: Pod
   179	metadata:
   180	  name: tf-gpu
   181	spec:
   182	  containers:
   183	  - name: gpu
   184	    image: tensorflow/tensorflow:2.0.1-gpu
   185	    command: [ "/bin/bash", "-ce", "tail -f /dev/null" ]
   186	    # ^ From 2.0.0 onwards, CMD is not set
   187	    imagePullPolicy: IfNotPresent
   188	    resources:
   189	      limits:
   190	        memory: 1024Mi
   191	        nvidia.com/gpu: 1 # requesting 1 GPU
   192	EOF
   193	
   194	# CUDA 9.1
   195	cat << EOF | kubectl create -f -
   196	apiVersion: v1
   197	kind: Pod
   198	metadata:
   199	  name: tf-gpu
   200	spec:
   201	  containers:
   202	  - name: gpu
   203	    image: tensorflow/tensorflow:1.9.0-gpu
   204	    imagePullPolicy: IfNotPresent
   205	    resources:
   206	      limits:
   207	        memory: 1024Mi
   208	        # ^ Set memory in case default limits are set low
   209	        nvidia.com/gpu: 1 # requesting 1 GPUs
   210	        # ^ For Legacy Accelerators mode this key must be renamed
   211	        #   'alpha.kubernetes.io/nvidia-gpu'
   212	  tolerations:
   213	  # This toleration will allow the gpu hook to run anywhere
   214	  #   By default this is permissive in case you have tainted your GPU nodes.
   215	  - operator: "Exists"
   216	  # ^ If you have a specific taint to target, comment out the above and modify
   217	  #   the example below
   218	
   219	### Example tolerations
   220	# - key: "dedicated"
   221	#   operator: "Equal"
   222	#   value: "gpu"
   223	#   effect: "NoExecute"
   224	EOF
   225	```
   226	
   227	#### Validate that GPUs are working
   228	
   229	```bash
   230	# Check that nodes are detected to have GPUs
   231	kubectl describe nodes | grep -E 'gpu:\s.*[1-9]'
   232	
   233	# Check the logs of the Tensorflow Container to ensure that it ran
   234	kubectl logs tf-gpu # no output since 2.0.0
   235	
   236	# Show GPU info from within the pod
   237	#   Only works in DevicePlugin mode
   238	kubectl exec -it tf-gpu nvidia-smi
   239	
   240	# Show Tensorflow detects GPUs from within the pod.
   241	#   Only works in DevicePlugin mode
   242	kubectl exec -it tf-gpu -- \
   243	  python -c 'from tensorflow.python.client import device_lib; print(device_lib.list_local_devices())'
   244	```

   252	```

    77	// PopulateInstanceGroupSpec sets default values in the InstanceGroup
    78	func PopulateInstanceGroupSpec(cluster *kops.Cluster, input *kops.InstanceGroup, cloud fi.Cloud, channel *kops.Channel) (*kops.InstanceGroup, error) {
    79	        klog.V(2).Infof("Populating instance group spec for %q", input.GetName())
    80	
    81	        var err error
    82	        err = validation.ValidateInstanceGroup(input, nil, false).ToAggregate()
    83	        if err != nil {
    84	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed validating input specs: %w", err)
    85	        }
    86	
    87	        ig := &kops.InstanceGroup{}
    88	        reflectutils.JSONMergeStruct(ig, input)
    89	
    90	        igSpec := &ig.Spec
    91	
    92	        // TODO: Clean up
    93	        if ig.IsControlPlane() {
    94	                if ig.Spec.MachineType == "" {
    95	                        ig.Spec.MachineType, err = defaultMachineType(cloud, cluster, ig)
    96	                        if err != nil {
    97	                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("assigning default machine type for control-plane nodes: %v", err)
    98	                        }
    99	
   100	                }
   101	                if ig.Spec.MinSize == nil {
   102	                        ig.Spec.MinSize = fi.PtrTo(int32(1))
   103	                }
   104	                if ig.Spec.MaxSize == nil {
   105	                        ig.Spec.MaxSize = fi.PtrTo(int32(1))
   106	                }
   107	        } else if ig.Spec.Role == kops.InstanceGroupRoleBastion {
   108	                if ig.Spec.MachineType == "" {
   109	                        ig.Spec.MachineType, err = defaultMachineType(cloud, cluster, ig)
   110	                        if err != nil {
   111	                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("error assigning default machine type for bastions: %v", err)
   112	                        }
   113	                }
   114	                if ig.Spec.MinSize == nil {
   115	                        ig.Spec.MinSize = fi.PtrTo(int32(1))
   116	                }
   117	                if ig.Spec.MaxSize == nil {
   118	                        ig.Spec.MaxSize = fi.PtrTo(int32(1))
   119	                }
   120	        } else {
   121	                if ig.IsAPIServerOnly() && !featureflag.APIServerNodes.Enabled() {
   122	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("apiserver nodes requires the APIServerNodes feature flag to be enabled")
   123	                }
   124	                if ig.Spec.MachineType == "" {
   125	                        ig.Spec.MachineType, err = defaultMachineType(cloud, cluster, ig)
   126	                        if err != nil {
   127	                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("error assigning default machine type for nodes: %v", err)
   128	                        }
   129	                }
   130	                if ig.Spec.MinSize == nil {
   131	                        ig.Spec.MinSize = fi.PtrTo(int32(2))
   132	                }
   133	                if ig.Spec.MaxSize == nil {
   134	                        ig.Spec.MaxSize = fi.PtrTo(int32(2))
   135	                }
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        if ig.Spec.Image == "" {
   139	                architecture, err := MachineArchitecture(cloud, ig.Spec.MachineType)
   140	                if err != nil {
   141	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("unable to determine machine architecture for InstanceGroup %q: %v", ig.ObjectMeta.Name, err)
   142	                }
   143	                ig.Spec.Image, err = defaultImage(cluster, channel, architecture)
   144	                if err != nil {
   145	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("unable to determine default image for instance group %q: %v", ig.ObjectMeta.Name, err)
   146	                }
   147	        }
   148	
   149	        if ig.Spec.Tenancy != "" && ig.Spec.Tenancy != "default" {
   150	                switch cluster.GetCloudProvider() {
   151	                case kops.CloudProviderAWS:
   152	                        if _, ok := awsDedicatedInstanceExceptions[ig.Spec.MachineType]; ok {
   153	                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("invalid dedicated instance type: %s", ig.Spec.MachineType)
   154	                        }
   155	                default:
   156	                        klog.Warning("Trying to set tenancy on non-AWS environment")
   157	                }
   158	        }
   159	
   160	        if ig.IsControlPlane() {
   161	                if len(ig.Spec.Subnets) == 0 {
   162	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("control-plane InstanceGroup %s did not specify any Subnets", ig.ObjectMeta.Name)
   163	                }
   164	        } else if ig.IsAPIServerOnly() && cluster.Spec.IsIPv6Only() {
   165	                if len(ig.Spec.Subnets) == 0 {
   166	                        for _, subnet := range cluster.Spec.Networking.Subnets {
   167	                                if subnet.Type != kops.SubnetTypePrivate && subnet.Type != kops.SubnetTypeUtility {
   168	                                        ig.Spec.Subnets = append(ig.Spec.Subnets, subnet.Name)
   169	                                }
   170	                        }
   171	                }
   172	        } else {
   173	                if len(ig.Spec.Subnets) == 0 {
   174	                        for _, subnet := range cluster.Spec.Networking.Subnets {
   175	                                if subnet.Type != kops.SubnetTypeDualStack && subnet.Type != kops.SubnetTypeUtility {
   176	                                        ig.Spec.Subnets = append(ig.Spec.Subnets, subnet.Name)
   177	                                }
   178	                        }
   179	                }
   180	
   181	                if len(ig.Spec.Subnets) == 0 {
   182	                        for _, subnet := range cluster.Spec.Networking.Subnets {
   183	                                if subnet.Type != kops.SubnetTypeUtility {
   184	                                        ig.Spec.Subnets = append(ig.Spec.Subnets, subnet.Name)
   185	                                }
   186	                        }
   187	                }
   188	        }
   189	
   190	        if len(ig.Spec.Subnets) == 0 {
   191	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("unable to infer any Subnets for InstanceGroup %s ", ig.ObjectMeta.Name)
   192	        }
   193	
   194	        hasGPU := false
   195	        clusterNvidia := false
   196	        if cluster.Spec.Containerd != nil && cluster.Spec.Containerd.NvidiaGPU != nil && fi.ValueOf(cluster.Spec.Containerd.NvidiaGPU.Enabled) {
   197	                clusterNvidia = true
   198	        }
   199	        igNvidia := false
   200	        if ig.Spec.Containerd != nil && ig.Spec.Containerd.NvidiaGPU != nil && fi.ValueOf(ig.Spec.Containerd.NvidiaGPU.Enabled) {
   201	                igNvidia = true
   202	        }
   203	
   204	        switch cluster.GetCloudProvider() {
   205	        case kops.CloudProviderAWS:
   206	                if clusterNvidia || igNvidia {
   207	                        mt, err := awsup.GetMachineTypeInfo(cloud.(awsup.AWSCloud), ec2types.InstanceType(ig.Spec.MachineType))
   208	                        if err != nil {
   209	                                return ig, fmt.Errorf("error looking up machine type info: %v", err)
   210	                        }
   211	                        hasGPU = mt.GPU
   212	                }
   213	        case kops.CloudProviderOpenstack:
   214	                if igNvidia {
   215	                        hasGPU = true
   216	                }
   217	        }
   218	
   219	        if hasGPU {
   220	                if ig.Spec.NodeLabels == nil {
   221	                        ig.Spec.NodeLabels = make(map[string]string)
   222	                }
   223	                ig.Spec.NodeLabels["kops.k8s.io/gpu"] = "1"
   224	                hasNvidiaTaint := false
   225	                for _, taint := range ig.Spec.Taints {
   226	                        if strings.HasPrefix(taint, "nvidia.com/gpu") {
   227	                                hasNvidiaTaint = true
   228	                        }
   229	                }
   230	                if !hasNvidiaTaint {
   231	                        ig.Spec.Taints = append(ig.Spec.Taints, "nvidia.com/gpu:NoSchedule")
   232	                }
   233	        }
   234	
   235	        if ig.Spec.Manager == "" {
   236	                ig.Spec.Manager = kops.InstanceManagerCloudGroup
   237	        }
   238	
   239	        if igSpec.Kubelet == nil {
   240	                igSpec.Kubelet = &kops.KubeletConfigSpec{}
   241	        }
   242	
   243	        var igKubeletConfig *kops.KubeletConfigSpec
   244	        // Start with the cluster kubelet config
   245	        if ig.IsControlPlane() {
   246	                if cluster.Spec.ControlPlaneKubelet != nil {
   247	                        igKubeletConfig = cluster.Spec.ControlPlaneKubelet.DeepCopy()
   248	                } else {
   249	                        igKubeletConfig = &kops.KubeletConfigSpec{}
   250	                }
   251	                // A few settings in Kubelet override those in ControlPlaneKubelet. I'm not sure why.
   252	                if cluster.Spec.Kubelet != nil && cluster.Spec.Kubelet.AnonymousAuth != nil && !*cluster.Spec.Kubelet.AnonymousAuth {
   253	                        igKubeletConfig.AnonymousAuth = fi.PtrTo(false)
   254	                }
   255	        } else {
   256	                if cluster.Spec.Kubelet != nil {
   257	                        igKubeletConfig = cluster.Spec.Kubelet.DeepCopy()
   258	                } else {
   259	                        igKubeletConfig = &kops.KubeletConfigSpec{}
   260	                }
   261	        }
   262	
   263	        // We include the NodeLabels in the userdata even for Kubernetes 1.16 and later so that
   264	        // rolling update will still replace nodes when they change.
   265	        nodeLabels, err := nodelabels.BuildNodeLabels(cluster, ig)
   266	        if err != nil {
   267	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("error building node labels: %w", err)
   268	        }
   269	        igKubeletConfig.NodeLabels = nodeLabels
   270	
   271	        useSecureKubelet := fi.ValueOf(igKubeletConfig.AnonymousAuth)
   272	
   273	        // While slices are overridden in most cases, taints are explicitly merged
   274	        taints := sets.NewString(igKubeletConfig.Taints...)
   275	        taints.Insert(igSpec.Taints...)
   276	        if ig.Spec.Kubelet != nil {
   277	                taints.Insert(igSpec.Kubelet.Taints...)
   278	        }
   279	        if cluster.Spec.Kubelet != nil {
   280	                taints.Insert(cluster.Spec.Kubelet.Taints...)
   281	        }
   282	        if ig.Spec.Kubelet != nil {
   283	                reflectutils.JSONMergeStruct(igKubeletConfig, ig.Spec.Kubelet)
   284	        }
   285	
   286	        {
   287	                if ig.IsControlPlane() {
   288	                        // (Even though the value is empty, we still expect <Key>=<Value>:<Effect>)
   289	                        taints.Insert(nodelabels.RoleLabelControlPlane20 + "=:" + string(v1.TaintEffectNoSchedule))
   290	                }
   291	                if ig.IsAPIServerOnly() {
   292	                        // (Even though the value is empty, we still expect <Key>=<Value>:<Effect>)
   293	                        taints.Insert(nodelabels.RoleLabelAPIServer16 + "=:" + string(v1.TaintEffectNoSchedule))
   294	                }
   295	        }
   296	
   297	        igKubeletConfig.Taints = taints.List()
   298	
   299	        if useSecureKubelet {
   300	                igKubeletConfig.AnonymousAuth = fi.PtrTo(false)
   301	        }
   302	
   303	        ig.Spec.Kubelet = igKubeletConfig
   304	
   305	        return ig, nil
   306	}
   307	
   308	// defaultMachineType returns the default MachineType for the instance group, based on the cloudprovider
   309	func defaultMachineType(cloud fi.Cloud, cluster *kops.Cluster, ig *kops.InstanceGroup) (string, error) {
   310	        switch cluster.GetCloudProvider() {
   311	        case kops.CloudProviderAWS:
   312	                if ig.Spec.Manager == kops.InstanceManagerKarpenter {
   313	                        return "", nil
   314	                }
   315	
   316	                instanceType, err := cloud.(awsup.AWSCloud).DefaultInstanceType(cluster, ig)
   317	                if err != nil {
   318	                        return "", fmt.Errorf("error finding default machine type: %v", err)
   319	                }
   320	                return instanceType, nil
   321	
   322	        case kops.CloudProviderGCE:
   323	                switch ig.Spec.Role {
   324	                case kops.InstanceGroupRoleControlPlane:
   325	                        return defaultMasterMachineTypeGCE, nil
   326	
   327	                case kops.InstanceGroupRoleNode:
   328	                        return defaultNodeMachineTypeGCE, nil
   329	
   330	                case kops.InstanceGroupRoleBastion:
   331	                        return defaultBastionMachineTypeGCE, nil
   332	                }
   333	
   334	        case kops.CloudProviderDO:
   335	                switch ig.Spec.Role {
   336	                case kops.InstanceGroupRoleControlPlane:
   337	                        return defaultMasterMachineTypeDO, nil
   338	
   339	                case kops.InstanceGroupRoleNode:
   340	                        return defaultNodeMachineTypeDO, nil
   341	
   342	                }
   343	
   344	        case kops.CloudProviderHetzner:
   345	                switch ig.Spec.Role {
   346	                case kops.InstanceGroupRoleControlPlane:
   347	                        return defaultMasterMachineTypeHetzner, nil
   348	
   349	                case kops.InstanceGroupRoleNode:
   350	                        return defaultNodeMachineTypeHetzner, nil
   351	
   352	                case kops.InstanceGroupRoleBastion:
   353	                        return defaultBastionMachineTypeHetzner, nil
   354	                }
   355	
   356	        case kops.CloudProviderOpenstack:
   357	                instanceType, err := cloud.(openstack.OpenstackCloud).DefaultInstanceType(cluster, ig)
   358	                if err != nil {
   359	                        return "", fmt.Errorf("error finding default machine type: %v", err)
   360	                }
   361	                return instanceType, nil
   362	
   363	        case kops.CloudProviderAzure:
   364	                switch ig.Spec.Role {
   365	                case kops.InstanceGroupRoleControlPlane:
   366	                        return defaultMasterMachineTypeAzure, nil
   367	
   368	                case kops.InstanceGroupRoleNode:
   369	                        return defaultNodeMachineTypeAzure, nil
   370	
   371	                case kops.InstanceGroupRoleBastion:
   372	                        return defaultBastionMachineTypeAzure, nil
   373	                }
   374	
   375	        case kops.CloudProviderScaleway:
   376	                switch ig.Spec.Role {
   377	                case kops.InstanceGroupRoleControlPlane:
   378	                        return defaultMasterMachineTypeScaleway, nil
   379	
   380	                case kops.InstanceGroupRoleNode:
   381	                        return defaultNodeMachineTypeScaleway, nil
   382	                }
   383	        }
   384	
   385	        klog.V(2).Infof("Cannot set default MachineType for CloudProvider=%q, Role=%q", cluster.GetCloudProvider(), ig.Spec.Role)
   386	        return "", nil
   387	}
   388

    25	// ContainerdOptionsBuilder adds options for containerd to the model
    26	type ContainerdOptionsBuilder struct {
    27	        *OptionsContext
    28	}
    29	
    30	var _ loader.ClusterOptionsBuilder = &ContainerdOptionsBuilder{}
    31	
    32	// BuildOptions is responsible for filling in the default setting for containerd daemon
    33	func (b *ContainerdOptionsBuilder) BuildOptions(o *kops.Cluster) error {
    34	        clusterSpec := &o.Spec
    35	
    36	        if clusterSpec.Containerd == nil {
    37	                clusterSpec.Containerd = &kops.ContainerdConfig{}
    38	        }
    39	
    40	        containerd := clusterSpec.Containerd
    41	
    42	        // Set version based on Kubernetes version
    43	        if fi.ValueOf(containerd.Version) == "" {
    44	                switch {
    45	                case b.IsKubernetesLT("1.27.2"):
    46	                        containerd.Version = fi.PtrTo("1.6.20")
    47	                        containerd.Runc = &kops.Runc{
    48	                                Version: fi.PtrTo("1.1.5"),
    49	                        }
    50	                default:
    51	                        containerd.Version = fi.PtrTo("1.7.25")
    52	                        containerd.Runc = &kops.Runc{
    53	                                Version: fi.PtrTo("1.2.4"),
    54	                        }
    55	                }
    56	        }
    57	        // Set default log level to INFO
    58	        containerd.LogLevel = fi.PtrTo("info")
    59	
    60	        if containerd.NvidiaGPU != nil && fi.ValueOf(containerd.NvidiaGPU.Enabled) && containerd.NvidiaGPU.DriverPackage == "" {
    61	                containerd.NvidiaGPU.DriverPackage = kops.NvidiaDefaultDriverPackage
    62	        }
    63	
    64	        return nil
    65	}

    40	const containerdConfigFilePath = "/etc/containerd/config.toml"
    41	
    42	// ContainerdBuilder install containerd (just the packages at the moment)
    43	type ContainerdBuilder struct {
    44	        *NodeupModelContext
    45	}
    46	
    47	var _ fi.NodeupModelBuilder = &ContainerdBuilder{}
    48	
    49	// Build is responsible for configuring the containerd daemon
    50	func (b *ContainerdBuilder) Build(c *fi.NodeupModelBuilderContext) error {
    51	        if b.skipInstall() {
    52	                klog.Infof("SkipInstall is set to true; won't install containerd")
    53	                return nil
    54	        }
    55	
    56	        installContainerd := true
    57	
    58	        // @check: neither flatcar nor containeros need provision containerd.service, just the containerd daemon options
    59	        switch b.Distribution {
    60	        case distributions.DistributionFlatcar:
    61	                klog.Infof("Detected Flatcar; won't install containerd")
    62	                installContainerd = false
    63	                b.buildSystemdServiceOverrideFlatcar(c)
    64	        case distributions.DistributionContainerOS:
    65	                klog.Infof("Detected ContainerOS; won't install containerd")
    66	                installContainerd = false
    67	                b.buildSystemdServiceOverrideContainerOS(c)
    68	        }
    69	
    70	        // Using containerd with Kubenet requires special configuration.
    71	        // This is a temporary backwards-compatible solution for kubenet users and will be deprecated when Kubenet is deprecated:
    72	        // https://github.com/containerd/containerd/blob/master/docs/cri/config.md#cni-config-template
    73	        if b.NodeupConfig.UsesKubenet {
    74	                if err := b.buildCNIConfigTemplateFile(c); err != nil {
    75	                        return err
    76	                }
    77	                if err := b.buildIPMasqueradeRules(c); err != nil {
    78	                        return err
    79	                }
    80	        }
    81	
    82	        // If there are containerd configuration overrides, apply them
    83	        if err := b.buildConfigFile(c); err != nil {
    84	                return err
    85	        }
    86	
    87	        if installContainerd {
    88	                if err := b.installContainerd(c); err != nil {
    89	                        return err
    90	                }
    91	        }
    92	
    93	        return nil
    94	}
    95	
    96	// installContainerd installs the binaries and services to run containerd.
    97	// We break it out because on immutable OSes we only configure containerd, we don't install it.
    98	func (b *ContainerdBuilder) installContainerd(c *fi.NodeupModelBuilderContext) error {
    99	        // Add Apache2 license
   100	        {
   101	                t := &nodetasks.File{
   102	                        Path:     "/usr/share/doc/containerd/apache.txt",
   103	                        Contents: fi.NewStringResource(resources.ContainerdApache2License),
   104	                        Type:     nodetasks.FileType_File,
   105	                }
   106	                c.AddTask(t)
   107	        }
   108	
   109	        // Add containerd binaries from containerd release package
   110	        f := b.Assets.FindMatches(regexp.MustCompile(`^bin/(containerd|ctr)`))
   111	        if len(f) == 0 {
   112	                // Add containerd binaries from containerd bundle package
   113	                f = b.Assets.FindMatches(regexp.MustCompile(`^(\./)?usr/local/bin/(containerd|crictl|ctr)`))
   114	        }
   115	        if len(f) == 0 {
   116	                // Add containerd binaries from Docker package (for ARM64 builds < v1.6.0)
   117	                // https://github.com/containerd/containerd/pull/6196
   118	                f = b.Assets.FindMatches(regexp.MustCompile(`^docker/(containerd|ctr)`))
   119	        }
   120	        if len(f) == 0 {
   121	                return fmt.Errorf("unable to find any containerd binaries in assets")
   122	        }
   123	        for k, v := range f {
   124	                fileTask := &nodetasks.File{
   125	                        Path:     filepath.Join("/usr/bin", k),
   126	                        Contents: v,
   127	                        Type:     nodetasks.FileType_File,
   128	                        Mode:     fi.PtrTo("0755"),
   129	                }
   130	                c.AddTask(fileTask)
   131	        }
   132	
   133	        // Add runc binary from https://github.com/opencontainers/runc
   134	        // https://github.com/containerd/containerd/issues/6541
   135	        f = b.Assets.FindMatches(regexp.MustCompile(`/runc\.(amd64|arm64)$`))
   136	        if len(f) == 0 {
   137	                // Add runc binary from containerd package (for builds < v1.6.0)
   138	                f = b.Assets.FindMatches(regexp.MustCompile(`^(\./)?usr/local/sbin/runc$`))
   139	        }
   140	        if len(f) == 0 {
   141	                // Add runc binary from Docker package (for ARM64 builds < v1.6.0)
   142	                // https://github.com/containerd/containerd/pull/6196
   143	                f = b.Assets.FindMatches(regexp.MustCompile(`^docker/runc$`))
   144	        }
   145	        if len(f) != 1 {
   146	                return fmt.Errorf("error finding runc asset")
   147	        }
   148	        for _, v := range f {
   149	                fileTask := &nodetasks.File{
   150	                        Path:     "/usr/sbin/runc",
   151	                        Contents: v,
   152	                        Type:     nodetasks.FileType_File,
   153	                        Mode:     fi.PtrTo("0755"),
   154	                }
   155	                c.AddTask(fileTask)
   156	        }
   157	
   158	        // Add configuration file for easier use of crictl
   159	        b.addCrictlConfig(c)
   160	
   161	        var containerdVersion string
   162	        if b.NodeupConfig.ContainerdConfig != nil {
   163	                containerdVersion = fi.ValueOf(b.NodeupConfig.ContainerdConfig.Version)
   164	        } else {
   165	                return fmt.Errorf("error finding contained version")
   166	        }
   167	        sv, err := semver.ParseTolerant(containerdVersion)
   168	        if err != nil {
   169	                return fmt.Errorf("error parsing container runtime version %q: %v", containerdVersion, err)
   170	        }
   171	        c.AddTask(b.buildSystemdService(sv))
   172	
   173	        if err := b.buildSysconfigFile(c); err != nil {
   174	                return err
   175	        }
   176	
   177	        return nil
   178	}
   179	
   180	func (b *ContainerdBuilder) buildSystemdService(containerdVersion semver.Version) *nodetasks.Service {
   181	        // Based on https://github.com/containerd/containerd/blob/master/containerd.service
   182	
   183	        manifest := &systemd.Manifest{}
   184	        manifest.Set("Unit", "Description", "containerd container runtime")
   185	        manifest.Set("Unit", "Documentation", "https://containerd.io")
   186	        manifest.Set("Unit", "After", "network.target local-fs.target")
   187	
   188	        manifest.Set("Service", "EnvironmentFile", "/etc/sysconfig/containerd")
   189	        manifest.Set("Service", "EnvironmentFile", "/etc/environment")
   190	        manifest.Set("Service", "ExecStartPre", "-/sbin/modprobe overlay")
   191	        manifest.Set("Service", "ExecStart", "/usr/bin/containerd -c "+containerdConfigFilePath+" \"$CONTAINERD_OPTS\"")
   192	
   193	        // notify the daemon's readiness to systemd
   194	        manifest.Set("Service", "Type", "notify")
   195	
   196	        // set delegate yes so that systemd does not reset the cgroups of containerd containers
   197	        manifest.Set("Service", "Delegate", "yes")
   198	        // kill only the containerd process, not all processes in the cgroup
   199	        manifest.Set("Service", "KillMode", "process")
   200	
   201	        manifest.Set("Service", "Restart", "always")
   202	        manifest.Set("Service", "RestartSec", "5")
   203	
   204	        manifest.Set("Service", "LimitNPROC", "infinity")
   205	        manifest.Set("Service", "LimitCORE", "infinity")
   206	        manifest.Set("Service", "LimitNOFILE", "1048576")
   207	        manifest.Set("Service", "TasksMax", "infinity")
   208	
   209	        // make killing of processes of this unit under memory pressure very unlikely
   210	        manifest.Set("Service", "OOMScoreAdjust", "-999")
   211	
   212	        manifest.Set("Install", "WantedBy", "multi-user.target")
   213	
   214	        if b.NodeupConfig.KubeletConfig.CgroupDriver == "systemd" {
   215	                cgroup := b.NodeupConfig.KubeletConfig.RuntimeCgroups
   216	                if cgroup != "" {
   217	                        manifest.Set("Service", "Slice", strings.Trim(cgroup, "/")+".slice")
   218	                }
   219	        }
   220	
   221	        manifestString := manifest.Render()
   222	        klog.V(8).Infof("Built service manifest %q\n%s", "containerd", manifestString)
   223	
   224	        service := &nodetasks.Service{
   225	                Name:       "containerd.service",
   226	                Definition: s(manifestString),
   227	        }
   228	
   229	        service.InitDefaults()
   230	
   231	        return service
   232	}
   233	
   234	// buildSystemdServiceOverrideContainerOS is responsible for overriding the containerd service for ContainerOS
   235	func (b *ContainerdBuilder) buildSystemdServiceOverrideContainerOS(c *fi.NodeupModelBuilderContext) {
   236	        lines := []string{
   237	                "[Service]",
   238	                "EnvironmentFile=/etc/environment",
   239	                "TasksMax=infinity",
   240	        }
   241	        contents := strings.Join(lines, "\n")
   242	
   243	        c.AddTask(&nodetasks.File{
   244	                Path:       "/etc/systemd/system/containerd.service.d/10-kops.conf",
   245	                Contents:   fi.NewStringResource(contents),
   246	                Type:       nodetasks.FileType_File,
   247	                AfterFiles: []string{containerdConfigFilePath},
   248	                OnChangeExecute: [][]string{
   249	                        {"systemctl", "daemon-reload"},
   250	                        {"systemctl", "restart", "containerd.service"},
   251	                        // We need to restart kops-configuration service since nodeup needs to load images
   252	                        // into containerd with the new config. We restart in the background because
   253	                        // kops-configuration is of type "one-shot", so the restart command will wait for
   254	                        // nodeup to finish executing.
   255	                        {"systemctl", "restart", "kops-configuration.service", "&"},
   256	                },
   257	        })
   258	}
   259	
   260	// buildSystemdServiceOverrideFlatcar is responsible for overriding the containerd service for Flatcar
   261	func (b *ContainerdBuilder) buildSystemdServiceOverrideFlatcar(c *fi.NodeupModelBuilderContext) {
   262	        lines := []string{
   263	                "[Service]",
   264	                "EnvironmentFile=/etc/environment",
   265	                "ExecStart=",
   266	                "ExecStart=/usr/bin/containerd --config " + containerdConfigFilePath,
   267	        }
   268	        contents := strings.Join(lines, "\n")
   269	
   270	        c.AddTask(&nodetasks.File{
   271	                Path:       "/etc/systemd/system/containerd.service.d/10-kops.conf",
   272	                Contents:   fi.NewStringResource(contents),
   273	                Type:       nodetasks.FileType_File,
   274	                AfterFiles: []string{containerdConfigFilePath},
   275	                OnChangeExecute: [][]string{
   276	                        {"systemctl", "daemon-reload"},
   277	                        {"systemctl", "restart", "containerd.service"},
   278	                        // We need to restart kops-configuration service since nodeup needs to load images
   279	                        // into containerd with the new config. We restart in the background because
   280	                        // kops-configuration is of type "one-shot", so the restart command will wait for
   281	                        // nodeup to finish executing.
   282	                        {"systemctl", "restart", "kops-configuration.service", "&"},
   283	                },
   284	        })
   285	}
   286	
   287	// buildSysconfigFile is responsible for creating the containerd sysconfig file
   288	func (b *ContainerdBuilder) buildSysconfigFile(c *fi.NodeupModelBuilderContext) error {
   289	        var containerd kops.ContainerdConfig
   290	        if b.NodeupConfig.ContainerdConfig != nil {
   291	                containerd = *b.NodeupConfig.ContainerdConfig
   292	        }
   293	
   294	        flagsString, err := flagbuilder.BuildFlags(&containerd)
   295	        if err != nil {
   296	                return fmt.Errorf("error building containerd flags: %v", err)
   297	        }
   298	
   299	        lines := []string{
   300	                "CONTAINERD_OPTS=" + flagsString,
   301	        }
   302	        contents := strings.Join(lines, "\n")
   303	
   304	        c.AddTask(&nodetasks.File{
   305	                Path:     "/etc/sysconfig/containerd",
   306	                Contents: fi.NewStringResource(contents),
   307	                Type:     nodetasks.FileType_File,
   308	        })
   309	
   310	        return nil
   311	}
   312	
   313	// buildConfigFile is responsible for creating the containerd configuration file
   314	func (b *ContainerdBuilder) buildConfigFile(c *fi.NodeupModelBuilderContext) error {
   315	        var config string
   316	
   317	        if b.NodeupConfig.ContainerdConfig != nil && b.NodeupConfig.ContainerdConfig.ConfigOverride != nil {
   318	                config = fi.ValueOf(b.NodeupConfig.ContainerdConfig.ConfigOverride)
   319	        } else {
   320	                if cc, err := b.buildContainerdConfig(); err != nil {
   321	                        return err
   322	                } else {
   323	                        config = cc
   324	                }
   325	        }
   326	        c.AddTask(&nodetasks.File{
   327	                Path:     containerdConfigFilePath,
   328	                Contents: fi.NewStringResource(config),
   329	                Type:     nodetasks.FileType_File,
   330	        })
   331	        return nil
   332	}
   333	
   334	// skipInstall determines if kops should skip the installation and configuration of containerd
   335	func (b *ContainerdBuilder) skipInstall() bool {
   336	        d := b.NodeupConfig.ContainerdConfig
   337	
   338	        // don't skip install if the user hasn't specified anything
   339	        if d == nil {
   340	                return false
   341	        }
   342	
   343	        return d.SkipInstall
   344	}

   346	// addCrictlConfig creates /etc/crictl.yaml, which lets crictl work out-of-the-box.
   347	func (b *ContainerdBuilder) addCrictlConfig(c *fi.NodeupModelBuilderContext) {
   348	        conf := `
   349	runtime-endpoint: unix:///run/containerd/containerd.sock
   350	`
   351	
   352	        c.AddTask(&nodetasks.File{
   353	                Path:     "/etc/crictl.yaml",
   354	                Contents: fi.NewStringResource(conf),
   355	                Type:     nodetasks.FileType_File,
   356	        })
   357	}
   358	
   359	// buildIPMasqueradeRules creates the DNAT rules.
   360	// Network modes where pods don't have "real network" IPs, use NAT so that they assume the IP of the node.
   361	func (b *ContainerdBuilder) buildIPMasqueradeRules(c *fi.NodeupModelBuilderContext) error {
   362	        // TODO: Should we just rely on running nodeup on every boot, instead of setting up a systemd unit?
   363	
   364	        if b.NodeupConfig.Networking.NonMasqueradeCIDR == "" {
   365	                // We could fall back to the pod CIDR, that is likely a good universal
   366	                klog.Infof("not setting up masquerade, as NonMasqueradeCIDR is not set")
   367	                return nil
   368	        }
   369	
   370	        if strings.HasSuffix(b.NodeupConfig.Networking.NonMasqueradeCIDR, "/0") {
   371	                klog.Infof("not setting up masquerade, as NonMasqueradeCIDR is %s", b.NodeupConfig.Networking.NonMasqueradeCIDR)
   372	                return nil
   373	        }
   374	
   375	        // This is based on rules from gce/cos/configure-helper.sh and the old logic in kubenet_linux.go
   376	
   377	        // We stick closer to the logic in kubenet_linux, both for compatibility, and because the GCE logic
   378	        // skips masquerading for all private CIDR ranges, but this depends on an assumption that is likely GCE-specific.
   379	        // On GCE custom routes are at the network level, on AWS they are at the route-table / subnet level.
   380	        // We cannot generally assume that because something is in the private network space, that it can reach us.
   381	        // If we adopt "native" pod IPs (GCP ip-alias, AWS VPC CNI, etc) we can likely move to rules closer to the upstream ones.
   382	        script := `#!/bin/bash
   383	# Built by kOps - do not edit
   384	
   385	iptables -w -t nat -N IP-MASQ
   386	iptables -w -t nat -A POSTROUTING -m comment --comment "ip-masq: ensure nat POSTROUTING directs all non-LOCAL destination traffic to our custom IP-MASQ chain" -m addrtype ! --dst-type LOCAL -j IP-MASQ
   387	iptables -w -t nat -A IP-MASQ -d {{.NonMasqueradeCIDR}} -m comment --comment "ip-masq: pod cidr is not subject to MASQUERADE" -j RETURN
   388	iptables -w -t nat -A IP-MASQ -m comment --comment "ip-masq: outbound traffic is subject to MASQUERADE (must be last in chain)" -j MASQUERADE
   389	`
   390	
   391	        script = strings.ReplaceAll(script, "{{.NonMasqueradeCIDR}}", b.NodeupConfig.Networking.NonMasqueradeCIDR)
   392	
   393	        c.AddTask(&nodetasks.File{
   394	                Path:     "/opt/kops/bin/cni-iptables-setup",
   395	                Contents: fi.NewStringResource(script),
   396	                Type:     nodetasks.FileType_File,
   397	                Mode:     s("0755"),
   398	        })
   399	
   400	        manifest := &systemd.Manifest{}
   401	        manifest.Set("Unit", "Description", "Configure iptables for kubernetes CNI")
   402	        manifest.Set("Unit", "Documentation", "https://github.com/kubernetes/kops")
   403	        manifest.Set("Unit", "Before", "network.target")
   404	        manifest.Set("Service", "Type", "oneshot")
   405	        manifest.Set("Service", "RemainAfterExit", "yes")
   406	        manifest.Set("Service", "ExecStart", "/opt/kops/bin/cni-iptables-setup")
   407	        manifest.Set("Install", "WantedBy", "basic.target")
   408	
   409	        manifestString := manifest.Render()
   410	        klog.V(8).Infof("Built service manifest %q\n%s", "cni-iptables-setup", manifestString)
   411	
   412	        service := &nodetasks.Service{
   413	                Name:       "cni-iptables-setup.service",
   414	                Definition: s(manifestString),
   415	        }
   416	        service.InitDefaults()
   417	        c.AddTask(service)
   418	
   419	        return nil
   420	}
   421	
   422	// buildCNIConfigTemplateFile is responsible for creating a special template for setups using Kubenet
   423	func (b *ContainerdBuilder) buildCNIConfigTemplateFile(c *fi.NodeupModelBuilderContext) error {
   424	        // Based on https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/blob/15a8a8ec4a3275a33b7f8eb3d4d98db2abad55b7/cluster/gce/gci/configure-helper.sh#L2911-L2937
   425	
   426	        contents := `{
   427	    "cniVersion": "0.4.0",
   428	    "name": "k8s-pod-network",
   429	    "plugins": [
   430	        {
   431	            "type": "ptp",
   432	            "ipam": {
   433	                "type": "host-local",
   434	                "ranges": [[{"subnet": "{{.PodCIDR}}"}]],
   435	                "routes": {{Routes}}
   436	            }
   437	        },
   438	        {
   439	            "type": "portmap",
   440	            "capabilities": {"portMappings": true}
   441	        }
   442	    ]
   443	}
   444	`
   445	
   446	        // We will gradually build up the schema here, as needed
   447	        type Route struct {
   448	                Dest string `json:"dst"`
   449	        }
   450	
   451	        routes := []Route{
   452	                {Dest: "0.0.0.0/0"},
   453	        }
   454	        if b.IsIPv6Only() {
   455	                routes = append(routes, Route{Dest: "::/0"})
   456	        }
   457	        routesJSON, err := json.Marshal(routes)
   458	        if err != nil {
   459	                return fmt.Errorf("building json: %w", err)
   460	        }
   461	        contents = strings.ReplaceAll(contents, "{{Routes}}", string(routesJSON))
   462

    53	// BootstrapChannelBuilder is responsible for handling the addons in channels
    54	type BootstrapChannelBuilder struct {
    55	        *model.KopsModelContext
    56	        ClusterAddons kubemanifest.ObjectList
    57	        Lifecycle     fi.Lifecycle
    58	        templates     *templates.Templates
    59	        assetBuilder  *assets.AssetBuilder
    60	}
    61	
    62	var _ fi.CloudupModelBuilder = &BootstrapChannelBuilder{}
    63	
    64	// networkingSelector is the labels set on networking addons
    65	//
    66	// The role.kubernetes.io/networking is used to label anything related to a networking addin,
    67	// so that if we switch networking plugins (e.g. calico -> weave or vice-versa), we'll replace the
    68	// old networking plugin, and there won't be old pods "floating around".
    69	//
    70	// This means whenever we create or update a networking plugin, we should be sure that:
    71	// 1. the selector is role.kubernetes.io/networking=1
    72	// 2. every object in the manifest is labeled with role.kubernetes.io/networking=1
    73	//
    74	// TODO: Some way to test/enforce this?
    75	//
    76	// TODO: Create "empty" configurations for others, so we can delete e.g. the kopeio configuration
    77	// if we switch to kubenet?
    78	//
    79	// TODO: Create configuration object for cni providers (maybe create it but orphan it)?
    80	//
    81	// NOTE: we try to suffix with -kops.1, so that we can increment versions even if the upstream version
    82	// hasn't changed.  The problem with semver is that there is nothing > 1.0.0 other than 1.0.1-pre.1
    83	func networkingSelector() map[string]string {
    84	        return map[string]string{"role.kubernetes.io/networking": "1"}
    85	}
    86	
    87	// NewBootstrapChannelBuilder creates a new BootstrapChannelBuilder
    88	func NewBootstrapChannelBuilder(modelContext *model.KopsModelContext,
    89	        clusterLifecycle fi.Lifecycle, assetBuilder *assets.AssetBuilder,
    90	        templates *templates.Templates,
    91	        addons kubemanifest.ObjectList,
    92	) *BootstrapChannelBuilder {
    93	        return &BootstrapChannelBuilder{
    94	                KopsModelContext: modelContext,
    95	                Lifecycle:        clusterLifecycle,
    96	                assetBuilder:     assetBuilder,
    97	                templates:        templates,
    98	                ClusterAddons:    addons,
    99	        }
   100	}

   306	type AddonList struct {
   307	        Items []*Addon
   308	}
   309	
   310	func (a *AddonList) Add(spec *channelsapi.AddonSpec) *Addon {
   311	        addon := &Addon{
   312	                Spec: spec,
   313	        }
   314	        a.Items = append(a.Items, addon)
   315	        return addon
   316	}

    27	// ContainerdConfig is the configuration for containerd
    28	type ContainerdConfig struct {
    29	        // Address of containerd's GRPC server (default "/run/containerd/containerd.sock").
    30	        Address *string `json:"address,omitempty" flag:"address"`
    31	        // ConfigAdditions adds additional config entries to the generated config file.
    32	        ConfigAdditions map[string]intstr.IntOrString `json:"configAdditions,omitempty"`
    33	        // ConfigOverride is the complete containerd config file provided by the user.
    34	        ConfigOverride *string `json:"configOverride,omitempty"`
    35	        // LogLevel controls the logging details [trace, debug, info, warn, error, fatal, panic] (default "info").
    36	        LogLevel *string `json:"logLevel,omitempty" flag:"log-level"`
    37	        // Packages overrides the URL and hash for the packages.
    38	        Packages *PackagesConfig `json:"packages,omitempty"`
    39	        // RegistryMirrors is list of image registries
    40	        RegistryMirrors map[string][]string `json:"registryMirrors,omitempty"`
    41	        // Root directory for persistent data (default "/var/lib/containerd").
    42	        Root *string `json:"root,omitempty" flag:"root"`
    43	        // SkipInstall prevents kOps from installing and modifying containerd in any way (default "false").
    44	        SkipInstall bool `json:"skipInstall,omitempty"`
    45	        // State directory for execution state files (default "/run/containerd").
    46	        State *string `json:"state,omitempty" flag:"state"`
    47	        // Version used to pick the containerd package.
    48	        Version *string `json:"version,omitempty"`
    49	        // NvidiaGPU configures the Nvidia GPU runtime.
    50	        NvidiaGPU *NvidiaGPUConfig `json:"nvidiaGPU,omitempty"`
    51	        // Runc configures the runc runtime.
    52	        Runc *Runc `json:"runc,omitempty"`
    53	        // SelinuxEnabled enables SELinux support
    54	        SeLinuxEnabled bool `json:"selinuxEnabled,omitempty"`
    55	        // NRI configures the Node Resource Interface.
    56	        NRI *NRIConfig `json:"nri,omitempty"`
    57	}
    58	
    59	type NRIConfig struct {
    60	        // Enable NRI support in containerd
    61	        Enabled *bool `json:"enabled,omitempty"`

    63	        PluginRegistrationTimeout *metav1.Duration `json:"pluginRegistrationTimeout,omitempty"`
    64	        // PluginRequestTimeout is the timeout for a plugin to handle a request

    66	}

    77	}

// DeepCopyInto is an autogenerated deepcopy function, copying the receiver, writing into out. in must be non-nil.
func (in *NvidiaGPUConfig) DeepCopyInto(out *NvidiaGPUConfig) {
	*out = *in
	if in.Enabled != nil {
		in, out := &in.Enabled, &out.Enabled
		*out = new(bool)
		**out = **in
	}
	if in.DCGMExporter != nil {
		in, out := &in.DCGMExporter, &out.DCGMExporter
		*out = new(DCGMExporterConfig)
		**out = **in
	}
	return
}

// DeepCopy is an autogenerated deepcopy function, copying the receiver, creating a new NvidiaGPUConfig.
func (in *NvidiaGPUConfig) DeepCopy() *NvidiaGPUConfig {
	if in == nil {
		return nil
	}
	out := new(NvidiaGPUConfig)
	in.DeepCopyInto(out)
	return out
}

def patch_nvidia_template():

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+
+import re
+
+def add_device_plugin_image_field():
+    # Read the file
+    with open('/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/containerdconfig.go', 'r') as f:
+        content = f.read()
+    
+    # Find the NvidiaGPUConfig struct and add the new field after DCGMExporter
+    pattern = r'(type NvidiaGPUConfig struct \{.*?// DCGMExporterConfig configures the DCGM exporter\s*DCGMExporter \*DCGMExporterConfig `json:"dcgmExporter,omitempty"`\s*\})'
+    
+    replacement = r'\1\n\t// DevicePluginImage is the image tag for the NVIDIA device plugin.\n\t// Default is "v0.12.2".\n\tDevicePluginImage *string `json:"devicePluginImage,omitempty"`'
+    
+    new_content = re.sub(pattern, replacement, content, flags=re.DOTALL)
+    
+    # Write the modified content back
+    with open('/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/containerdconfig.go', 'w') as f:
+        f.write(new_content)
+

+

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+
+import re
+
+def patch_nvidia_template():
+    # Read the template
+    with open('/testbed/upup/models/cloudup/resources/addons/nvidia.addons.k8s.io/k8s-1.16.yaml.template', 'r') as f:
+        content = f.read()
+    
+    # Replace the hardcoded image tag with a template variable
+    pattern = r'image: nvcr\.io/nvidia/k8s-device-plugin:v0\.12\.2'
+    replacement = 'image: nvcr.io/nvidia/k8s-device-plugin:{{ with .Containerd.NvidiaGPU.DevicePluginImage }}{{ . }}{{ else }}v0.12.2{{ end }}'
+    
+    new_content = re.sub(pattern, replacement, content)
+    
+    # Write the modified template back
+    with open('/testbed/upup/models/cloudup/resources/addons/nvidia.addons.k8s.io/k8s-1.16.yaml.template', 'w') as f:
+        f.write(new_content)
+    
+    print("Patched NVIDIA device plugin template to support configurable image tag")
+    print("Now the image tag can be configured using .DevicePluginImage field")
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    patch_nvidia_template()
